              <ul class="cf" id="cms_fragment_4396_ul">
               <li class="cf aid0 " id="cms_fragment_4396_1">
                <div>
                 <div class="pic">
                  <a href="http://bbs.tianya.cn/post-754-11910-1.shtml" id="cms_fragment_4396_1_img_link" name="title-link" target="_blank" title="没吃过这些美食就不算来过琼海">

                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="summary-title">
                  <span class="subject">
                   <a desc="标题" href="http://bbs.tianya.cn/post-754-11910-1.shtml" id="cms_fragment_4396_1_title" target="_blank" title="没吃过这些美食就不算来过琼海">
                    没吃过这些美食就不算来过琼海
                   </a>
                  </span>

                 <div class="summary">
